callbacks = []
filepath="./weights/model-{epoch:02d}-{val_loss:.5f}.h5"
callback_save = keras.callbacks.ModelCheckpoint(filepath, monitor='val_loss',
                                                verbose=0, save_best_only=True,
                                                save_weights_only=False, mode='auto', period=1)
#callback_tensorboard = keras.callbacks.TensorBoard(log_dir='./logs', histogram_freq=0, batch_size=batch_size, write_graph=False,
#                            write_grads=False, write_images=False,
#                            embeddings_freq=0, embeddings_layer_names=None, embeddings_metadata=None)
csv_logger = CSVLogger('./logs/log.csv', append=False, separator=';')
if export_model is True:
    callbacks.append(callback_save)
    #callbacks.append(callback_tensorboard)
if export_history is True:
    callbacks.append(csv_logger)
In [18]:
# https://machinelearningmastery.com/custom-metrics-deep-learning-keras-python/
# https://github.com/keras-team/keras/blob/master/keras/metrics.py
def acc_sign(y_true, y_pred):
    return K.mean(K.equal(K.sign(y_pred), y_true), axis=-1)

def acc_round(y_true, y_pred):
    # each interval for class -1, 0, 1 must have a width of 2/3 to be equally distributed
    # therefore you must convert (1/3) to (1/2) and only then round to the closest integer
    # 1/3 * x = 1/2
    return K.mean(K.equal(K.round(y_pred * 1.5), y_true), axis=-1)

Compile the model¶

https://towardsdatascience.com/learning-rate-schedules-and-adaptive-learning-rate-methods-for-deep-learning-2c8f433990d1 https://shaoanlu.wordpress.com/2017/05/29/sgd-all-which-one-is-the-best-optimizer-dogs-vs-cats-toy-experiment/

def step_decay(epoch): initial_lrate = 0.2 drop = 0.1 epochs_drop = 10.0 lrate = initial_lrate * math.pow(drop,
math.floor((1+epoch)/epochs_drop)) return lrate

lrate = LearningRateScheduler(step_decay)

callbacks.append(lrate)¶

In [19]:
#optimizer = SGD(lr=0.2, decay=0, momentum=0.9, nesterov=True)
optimizer = Adam(lr=0.001, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=1e-08, decay=0.0, clipnorm=None)

model.compile(loss=['mean_squared_error', 'categorical_crossentropy'],
              optimizer=optimizer, loss_weights={'value': 0.5, 'policy': 0.5}, 
                     metrics=[acc_sign, 'acc'], callbacks=callbacks)

In [23]:
t_s = time()
# set a custom seed for reproducability
random.seed(42)

# define a list which describes the order of the processed batches
ordering = list(range(nb_parts))

hist = []
for e in range(nb_epoch):
    logging.info("EPOCH %d/%d", e+1, nb_epoch)
    logging.info("=========================")
                 
    # reshuffle the ordering of the training game batches (shuffle works in place)
    random.shuffle(ordering)
    
    for i, part_id in enumerate(ordering):
        logging.info('part id %d', part_id)
        
        # load one chunk of the dataset from memory
        s_idcs_train, x_train, yv_train, yp_train, pgn_datasets_train = load_pgn_dataset(part_id=part_id)

        # only evaluate on the last part of the epoch
        #if i == len(ordering)-1:
        ## add the history to the full history
        hist_cur = model.fit(x_train, [yv_train, yp_train],
                         validation_data=(x_test, [yv_test, yp_test]), epochs=1, batch_size=batch_size)
        
        hist.append(hist_cur)

print('Elapsed time for training(hh:mm:ss): ' + str(datetime.timedelta(seconds=round(time() - t_s))))

Show the training progress¶

Create a summary history of the training progress¶

In [36]:
epochs_plt = np.linspace(0, nb_epoch, num=len(hist))
hist_loss = []
hist_val_loss = []
hist_value_acc_sign = []
hist_val_value_acc_sign = []
hist_policy_acc = []
hist_val_policy_acc = []

for hist_cur in hist:
    hist_loss.append(hist_cur.history['loss'][0])
    hist_val_loss.append(hist_cur.history['val_loss'][0])
    hist_value_acc_sign.append(hist_cur.history['value_acc_sign'][0])
    hist_val_value_acc_sign.append(hist_cur.history['val_value_acc_sign'][0])
    hist_policy_acc.append(hist_cur.history['policy_acc'][0])
    hist_val_policy_acc.append(hist_cur.history['val_policy_acc'][0])

Evaluate Performance¶

In [49]:
def eval_pos(x_mate, yp_mate, verbose=False):
    
    board = get_mat_of_current_board(x_mate)
    if verbose is True:
        print("{0}'s turn".format(chess.COLOR_NAMES[board.turn]))
        print("black/white {0}".format(board.pockets))
    pred = model.predict(np.expand_dims(x_mate, axis=0))

    true_mat = yp_mate.reshape(78,8,8)
    true_move = filter_moves(board, true_mat, is_white_to_move=board.turn, renormalize_confidences=False)[0][0]
    
    pred_mat = pred[1][0].reshape(78,8,8)
    opts = 5
    pred_moves = filter_moves(board, pred_mat, is_white_to_move=board.turn, renormalize_confidences=False)[0][:opts]

    legal_move_cnt = board.legal_moves.count()
    mate_move_cnt = str(board.legal_moves).count('#')
    
    is_mate_5_top = False
    
    for pred_move in pred_moves:
        board_5_top = deepcopy(board)
        board_5_top.push(pred_move)
        if board_5_top.is_checkmate() is True:
            is_mate_5_top = True
            break
    
    board.push(pred_moves[0])
    
    is_checkmate = False
    if board.is_checkmate() is True:
        is_checkmate = True
        
    # somehow we must mirror the move for white ?!
    #if board.turn == chess.WHITE:
    #    true_move = mirror_move(true_move)
    #    for i, pred_move in enumerate(pred_moves):
    #        pred_moves[i] = mirror_move(pred_move)
        
    filtered_pred = sorted(pred[1][0], reverse=True)
    
    if verbose is True:
        plt.barh(range(opts)[::-1], filtered_pred[:opts])
        ax = plt.gca()
        ax.set_yticks(range(opts)[::-1])
        ax.set_yticklabels(pred_moves)
        plt.title('True Move:' + str(true_move) +
                 '\nEval:' + str(pred[0][0]))
        plt.show()
    
    return pred, pred_moves, true_move, board, is_checkmate, is_mate_5_top, legal_move_cnt, mate_move_cnt

nb_pos = len(x_mate)
mates_found = []
mates_5_top_found = []
legal_mv_cnts = []
mate_mv_cnts = []

for i in range(nb_pos):
    pred, pred_moves, true_move, board, is_mate, is_mate_5_top, legal_mv_cnt, mate_mv_cnt= eval_pos(x_mate[i], yp_mate[i])
    mates_found.append(is_mate)
    legal_mv_cnts.append(legal_mv_cnt)
    mate_mv_cnts.append(mate_mv_cnt)
    mates_5_top_found.append(is_mate_5_top)

def clean_string(np_string):
    string = str(site_mate[i]).replace("b'", "")
    string = string.replace("'", "")
    string = string.replace('"', '')
    
    return string
